						Great to read this old cl ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						Great to read this old classic once again.  The story keeps you interested in the southern way of life in the early years of the depression in Alabama.  I quickly felt myself in this small town atmosphere through the eyes of a young &quot;Jem.&quot;  I grew up in a place like this, and was curious and scared of a man just like Boo Radley.  The strength of Atticus for the community and fellow man begins an era that will see changes for those who were discriminated back in that day.  Absolutely loved to read this again, since it has been many years.  Highly recommended!
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>

						I work as an early childhood educator and always purchase Brown Bear books as gifts for parents in our program to read to their children. This book has a wonderful cadence and rythmn that can be tapped on the board book when read to the child. This is a great way to keep the childs attention while reading the book. It is also exciting when you see the child pick up the book and start tapping and &quot;reading&quot; (as best they can) the book. It also teachers children primary colors and is easily memorized for retelling. I recommend it to everyone with young children - and for gifts.

			<div class="user-review-heading">A touching thing that doesn't sugar coat things.</div>
			
				<div class="review-text">
					<p class="review-text-half">
						
						Oh goodness. Where to sta ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						Oh goodness. Where to start. This book was certainly not what I expected when I started it, but I was not disappointed. It really got into my head, and made me think a lot in general. The book had me sobbing uncontrollably by the end, and long after I was finished the tears continued. A great read.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>
					</p>
				</div>
